    <Options>
      <Option key="XmlEncoding"/>
      <Option key="TimeStampOutputFormat">%M-%D-%Y %H:%I:%S.%f %A</Option>
      <Option key="DateTimeOutputFormat">%M-%D-%Y %H:%I:%S %A</Option>
      <Option key="OutputEncoding">UTF-8</Option>
      <Option key="DefaultEmptyNumericsToZero">FALSE</Option>
      <Option key="AddTZIndicators">true</Option>
      <Option key="AddVendorMnemonic">true</Option>
      <Option key="SendNullMacro"/>
    </Options>
    <MappingFragments/>
    <OutputDef>
      <Block displayName="Initial store of variables">
        <ForEach displayName="Find and Store Bond Structure" recordType="cmfAsset.unvalidatedAsset.description">
          <Do>
            <If>
              <expr><![CDATA[return cmfAsset.unvalidatedAsset.description.TYPE == "Bond Structure";]]></expr>
              <Then>
                <Execute>
                  <expr><![CDATA[return StoreString("BondStructureStrVal", cmfAsset.unvalidatedAsset.description);]]></expr>
                </Execute>
              </Then>
              <Else/>
            </If>
          </Do>
        </ForEach>
        <ForEach displayName="Find and Store Series value" recordType="cmfAsset.unvalidatedAsset.identifiers.identifier">
          <Do>
            <If>
              <expr><![CDATA[return cmfAsset.unvalidatedAsset.identifiers.identifier.TYPE == "Series";]]></expr>
              <Then>
                <Execute>
                  <expr><![CDATA[return StoreString("SeriesStrVal", cmfAsset.unvalidatedAsset.identifiers.identifier);]]></expr>
                </Execute>
              </Then>
              <Else/>
            </If>
          </Do>
        </ForEach>
        <ForEach displayName="Find and Store Redemption Value" recordType="cmfAsset.unvalidatedAsset.principalDetail.principalEvent">
          <Do>
            <If>
              <expr><![CDATA[return cmfAsset.unvalidatedAsset.principalDetail.principalEvent.PRINCIPAL_EVENT_TYPE == "Redemption";]]></expr>
              <Then>
                <Execute>
                  <expr><![CDATA[return StoreString("RedemptionStrVal", cmfAsset.unvalidatedAsset.principalDetail.principalEvent.principalEventTerm.FIXED_RATE);]]></expr>
                </Execute>
              </Then>
              <Else/>
            </If>
          </Do>
        </ForEach>
        <ForEach displayName="Find and store BBUnique and MTN ID" recordType="cmfAsset.unvalidatedAsset.identifiers.identifier">
          <Do>
            <Execute displayName="Store BBUNIQUE">
              <expr><![CDATA[if (Strcmp(cmfAsset.unvalidatedAsset.identifiers.identifier.TYPE, "BBUNIQUE"))
	return StoreString("BBUNIQUEStrVal", cmfAsset.unvalidatedAsset.identifiers.identifier);
else
	return "";]]></expr>
            </Execute>
            <Execute displayName="Store MZHMTNREF">
              <expr><![CDATA[if (Strcmp(cmfAsset.unvalidatedAsset.identifiers.identifier.TYPE, "MZHMTNREF"))
	return StoreString("MZHMTNREFStrVal", cmfAsset.unvalidatedAsset.identifiers.identifier);
else
	return "";]]></expr>
            </Execute>
          </Do>
        </ForEach>
        <ForEach displayName="Find and store UriDashi" recordType="cmfAsset.unvalidatedAsset.group">
          <Do>
            <If>
              <expr><![CDATA[return Strcmp(cmfAsset.unvalidatedAsset.group.PARENT_GROUP_NAME, "Uridashi");]]></expr>
              <Then>
                <Execute>
                  <expr><![CDATA[return StoreString("UriDashiStrVal", cmfAsset.unvalidatedAsset.group);]]></expr>
                </Execute>
              </Then>
              <Else/>
            </If>
          </Do>
        </ForEach>
        <Execute displayName=":EMTN">
          <expr><![CDATA[if (Strcmp("N", "Y"))
	return StoreString("BONDTYP1", "EURTRMNTE_");
else
	return StoreString("BONDTYP1", "NONEURTRMNTE_");]]></expr>
        </Execute>
        <Execute displayName=":MTN">
          <expr><![CDATA[if (Strcmp(cmfAsset.unvalidatedAsset.assetName.SUBTYPE, "MTN"))
	return StoreString("BONDTYP2", "MTNNOTE_");
else
	return StoreString("BONDTYP2", "NONMTNNOTE_");]]></expr>
        </Execute>
        <Execute displayName=":BRADY">
          <expr><![CDATA[if (Strcmp("N", "Y"))
	return StoreString("BONDTYP3", "BRADY_");
else
	return StoreString("BONDTYP3", "NONBRADY_");]]></expr>
        </Execute>
        <Execute displayName="Concat">
          <expr><![CDATA[return StoreString("BONDTYP", Strcat(GetStringByKey("BONDTYP1"), Strcat(GetStringByKey("BONDTYP2"), Strcat(GetStringByKey("BONDTYP3"), ""))));]]></expr>
        </Execute>
        <Execute displayName="Maturity Date">
          <expr><![CDATA[if (FieldPresent(cmfAsset.unvalidatedAsset.assetName.MATURITY_DATE))
	return StoreString("MatDateVal", cmfAsset.unvalidatedAsset.assetName.MATURITY_DATE);
else
	return "";]]></expr>
        </Execute>
        <Execute displayName="Issue Currency">
          <expr><![CDATA[if (FieldPresent(cmfAsset.unvalidatedAsset.assetName.ISSUE_CURRENCY))
	return StoreString("IssueCurrencyVal", cmfAsset.unvalidatedAsset.assetName.ISSUE_CURRENCY);
else
	return "";]]></expr>
        </Execute>
        <Execute displayName="Coupon Currency">
          <expr><![CDATA[if (FieldPresent(cmfAsset.unvalidatedAsset.incomeDetail.couponDetail.couponTerm.COUPON_CURRENCY))
	return StoreString("CouponCurrencyVal", cmfAsset.unvalidatedAsset.incomeDetail.couponDetail.couponTerm.COUPON_CURRENCY);
else
	return "";]]></expr>
        </Execute>
      </Block>
      <If displayName="Check if Mandatory fields exist">
        <expr><![CDATA[return AllHaveValue(cmfAsset.unvalidatedAsset.assetName, cmfAsset.unvalidatedAsset.assetName.ISSUE_DATE, GetStringByKey("MZHMTNREFStrVal"), GetStringByKey("MatDateVal"), cmfAsset.unvalidatedAsset.principalDetail.CALLABLE_BY_ISSUER, cmfAsset.unvalidatedAsset.incomeDetail.couponDetail.COUPON_TYPE, cmfAsset.unvalidatedAsset.incomeDetail.couponDetail.couponTerm.DAY_COUNT_BASIS, GetStringByKey("UriDashiStrVal"), cmfAsset.unvalidatedAsset.assetName.CURRENT_NOMINAL);]]></expr>
